# ::id 13973-he-IL
# ::en_utt what movies has [person : neil walker] done
# ::annot_utt איזה סרטים [person : גל גדות] עשתה
# ::snt איזה סרטים גל גדות עשתה
(d / do-02
      :ARG0 (p / person :name (n / name :op1 "גל" :op2 "גדות"))
      :ARG1 (m / movie :plural +
            :mod (a / amr-unknown)))

# ::annot_utt 請用 google 搜索拉什莫爾山的位置和資訊
# ::snt 請用 google 搜索拉什莫爾山的位置和資訊
(g / google-01 :mode imperative :polite +
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (a / and
            :op1 (l2 / location
                  :location-of (l / location :name (n / name :op1 "mount" :op2 "rushmore")))
            :op2 (i3 / information
                  :topic l)))

# ::annot_utt sök ord synonym
# ::snt sök ord synonym
(s2 / search-01 :mode imperative
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG2 (s / synonym
            :mod (w / word)))

# ::id 14797-he-IL
# ::en_utt what is the stock information of [business_name : walmart]
# ::annot_utt מה מידע המניה של [business_name : שופרסל]
# ::snt מה מידע המניה של שופרסל
(i3 / information
      :topic (s / stock
            :mod (c / company :name (n / name :op1 "שופרסל")))
      :mod (a / amr-unknown))

(a / amr-choice
      :op1 (u / up-02
            :ARG1 (t / thing
                  :ARG2-of (p / price-01
                        :ARG1 (s / stock

      :op2 (d / down-03
            :ARG1 t))

# ::annot_utt ما الذي يفعله [person : باراك أوباما] الآن
# ::snt ما الذي يفعله باراك أوباما الآن
(d / do-02
      :ARG0 (p / person :name (n / name :op1 "باراك" :op2 "أوباما"))
      :ARG1 (a / amr-unknown)
      :time (n2 / now
            :degree (r / right-yy)))

# ::snt តើ ហ៊ុន សែន កំពុងធ្វើអ្វីឥឡូវនេះ
(d / do-02
      :ARG0 (p / person :name (n / name :op1 "ហ៊ុន" :op2 "សែន"))
      :ARG1 (a / amr-unknown)
      :time (n2 / now
            :degree (r / right-yy)))

# ::annot_utt எத்தனை பந்துவீச்சு பந்து
# ::snt எத்தனை பந்துவீச்சு பந்து
(c / cost-01
      :ARG1 (b / ball
            :purpose (b2 / bowl-01))
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::id 13438-he-IL
# ::en_utt how are my stocks doing [date : today]
# ::annot_utt איך המניות שלי [date : היום]
# ::snt איך המניות שלי היום
(d / do-02
      :ARG0 (s / stock
            :poss (i / i))
      :manner (a / amr-unknown)
      :time (t / today))

# ::snt өнөөдөр миний хувьцаанууд юу болж байна
(d / do-02
      :ARG0 (s / stock
            :poss (i / i))
      :manner (a / amr-unknown)
      :time (t / today))

# ::snt jello shots တွေက ကယ်လိုရီမပါဘူးလား
(f / free-01
      :ARG1 (s / shot
            :consist-of (f2 / food-dish :name (n / name :op1 "jell")))
      :ARG2 (c / calorie)
      :polarity (a / amr-unknown))

# ::snt в каких фильмах играла елизавета боярская
(p / play-02
      :ARG0 (p2 / person :name (n / name :op1 "елизавета" :op2 "боярская"))
      :subevent-of (m / movie :plural +
            :mod (a / amr-unknown)))

# ::annot_utt תגיד לי למי יש את הלהיט מספר אחת במצעד הלהיטים טופ עשרים
# ::snt תגיד לי למי יש את הלהיט מספר אחת במצעד הלהיטים טופ עשרים

                              :ord (o / ordinal-entity :value 1))
                        :ARG1-of (h2 / have-quant-91
                              :ARG3 (m / most)
                              :ARG5 (p2 / person
                                    :ARG0-of (h3 / hit-07
                                          :ARG2 (p3 / publication :name (n / name :op1 "billboard" :op2 "top" :op3 "twenty"))))))))
      :ARG2 (i / i))

# ::annot_utt tell me who has the most number one hits on the billboard top twenty
# ::snt tell me who has the most number one hits on the billboard top twenty
(t / tell-01 :mode imperative
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (p / person
            :ARG0-of (h / have-03
                  :ARG1 (t2 / thing
                        :ARG1-of (h5 / hit-07
                              :ord (o / ordinal-entity :value 1))
                        :ARG1-of (h2 / have-quant-91
                              :ARG3 (m / most)
                              :ARG5 (p2 / person
                                    :ARG0-of (h3 / hit-07
                                          :ARG2 (p3 / publication :name (n / name :op1 "billboard" :op2 "top" :op3 "twenty"))))))))
      :ARG2 (i / i))

# ::snt биллбоардын шилдэг хорьд хэн хамгийн их хит болж байгааг надад хэлээч
(t / tell-01 :mode imperative
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (p / person
            :ARG0-of (h / have-03
                  :ARG1 (t2 / thing
                        :ARG1-of (h5 / hit-07
                              :ord (o / ordinal-entity :value 1))
                        :ARG1-of (h2 / have-quant-91
                              :ARG3 (m / most)
                              :ARG5 (p2 / person
                                    :ARG0-of (h3 / hit-07
                                          :ARG2 (p3 / publication :name (n / name :op1 "billboard" :op2 "top" :op3 "twenty"))))))))
      :ARG2 (i / i))

                        :ARG0 p
                        :ARG1 (i / i)

                        :ARG1-of (b / back-01)))

# ::annot_utt [place_name : বরিশাল] জনসংখ্যা কত
# ::snt বরিশাল জনসংখ্যা কত
(p / populate-01
      :ARG1 (s / state :name (n / name :op1 "বরিশাল"))
      :ARG2 (p2 / person
            :quant (a / amr-unknown)))

      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (b / book :plural +

                        :ARG1-of (f / favor-01)))
            :mod (l2 / last)))

# ::annot_utt ఇష్టమైన రచయితలు ప్రచురించిన తాజా పుస్తకాలను జాబితా చేయండి

(l / list-01 :mode imperative
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (b / book :plural +
            :ARG1-of (p / publish-01
                  :ARG0 (p2 / person :plural +
                        :ARG0-of (a / author-01)
                        :ARG1-of (f / favor-01)))
            :mod (l2 / last)))

(e / equal-01
      :ARG1 (s / sum-of :op1 4 :op2 6)
      :ARG2 (a / amr-unknown))

# ::snt ಈ ಮೌಲ್ಯಗಳ ಆಧಾರದ ಮೇಲೆ ಓಮ್ನ ನಿಯಮವನ್ನು ಲೆಕ್ಕಹಾಕಿ
(c / calculate-01 :mode imperative
      :ARG0 (y / you)
      :ARG1 (e / empirical-law :name (n / name :op1 "ohm's" :op2 "law"))
      :ARG1-of (b / base-02
            :ARG2 (t / thing :plural +
                  :ARG2-of (v / value-01)
                  :mod (t2 / this))))

# ::annot_utt האם [place_name : אשקלון] נמצאת ליד [place_name : אשדוד]
# ::snt האם אשקלון נמצאת ליד אשדוד

      :ARG1 (c / city :name (n2 / name :op1 "אשקלון"))
      :ARG2 (c2 / city :name (n3 / name :op1 "אשדוד"))
      :polarity (a / amr-unknown))
